linguas="af an ar ast az be bg bn bo br bs ca ca@valencia ckb cs da de el en_AU en_CA en_GB eo es et eu fa fi fo fr fy gd gl gu he hi hr hu ia id is it ja kk km kn ko ku lb lt lv mhr mi ml mr ms my nb nl nn oc pa pl pt_BR pt ro ru sc sd shn si sk sl sq sr sv ta te tg th tl tr ug uk uz vi wae zh_CN zh_HK zh_TW "; \
for lang in $linguas; do \
  dir=/usr/src/tmp/lightdm-buildroot/usr/share/locale/$lang/LC_MESSAGES; \
  /bin/sh /usr/src/RPM/BUILD/lightdm-1.32.0/install-sh -d $dir; \
  if test -r $lang.gmo; then \
    /usr/bin/ginstall -c -m 644 $lang.gmo $dir/lightdm.mo; \
    echo "installing $lang.gmo as $dir/lightdm.mo"; \
  else \
    /usr/bin/ginstall -c -m 644 ./$lang.gmo $dir/lightdm.mo; \
    echo "installing ./$lang.gmo as" \
	 "$dir/lightdm.mo"; \
  fi; \
  if test -r $lang.gmo.m; then \
    /usr/bin/ginstall -c -m 644 $lang.gmo.m $dir/lightdm.mo.m; \
    echo "installing $lang.gmo.m as $dir/lightdm.mo.m"; \
  else \
    if test -r ./$lang.gmo.m ; then \
      /usr/bin/ginstall -c -m 644 ./$lang.gmo.m \
	$dir/lightdm.mo.m; \
      echo "installing ./$lang.gmo.m as" \
	   "$dir/lightdm.mo.m"; \
    else \
      true; \
    fi; \
  fi; \
done
